0                                  14816              *
                                   14817              *  LINE NUMBER RECOGNITION ROUTINE DELETED !!,
                                   14818              *  LINE NUMBERS NOW RECOGNIZED BY SCANNER !!
                                   14819              *
                                   14820              *  line numbers (symbolic ones too) are now recognized by
                                   14821              *  by the scanner.  use the SYMLN flag.  (eg SCKW ,ROUTINE,SYMLN ).
                                   14822              *  the processing routine will be entered with R0 - line number,
                                   14823              *  R1 - delta.  go for it.
                                   14824              *
                                   14825              *  what follows are the old LNENOPRT comments.  Remove in 1991.
                                   14826              *
                                   14827              * ----------------------------------------------------------
                                   14828              *
                                   14829              * to use this prt, register r6 must be set to the desired
                                   14830              * return address if a line number is recognized
                                   14831              *
                                   14832              * R0 contains the specified line number on exit
                                   14833              * R1 has a delta that can be used by collect, move and copy
                                   14834              * R15 has return codes to show which way the line no was
                                   14835              * specified.
                                   14836              * R15 -  0 regular line number specified
                                   14837              *        4 first specified
                                   14838              *        8 current specified
                                   14839              *       12 last specified
                                   14840              *       16 end specified
                                   14841              *       20 next specified
                                   14842              *       24 previous specified
                                   14843              *       28 return specified
                                   14844              *       32 ATTN specified
                                   14845              *       36 ABORT specified
                                   14846              *
                                   14847              * after the line number specified has been processed,
                                   14848              * an increment is scanned for and added in if found
                                   14849              * unless cpfnoinc bit is on in cplflg4.
                                   14850              *
                                   14851              *         ENTRY LNENOPRT,LNENOPRN
                                   14852              *LNENOPRT SCKW  F,SCNFRST
                                   14853              *         SCKW  L,SCNLAST
                                   14854              *         SCKW  RETURN,SCNRETN,A
                                   14855              *LNENOPRN SCKW  ,SCNLNENO,LN
                                   14856              *         SCKW  FIRST,SCNFRST,A
                                   14857              *         SCKW  CURRENT,SCNCURR,A
                                   14858              *         SCKW  LAST,SCNLAST,A
                                   14859              *         SCKW  END,SCNEND
                                   14860              *         SCKW  NEXT,SCNNEXT,A
                                   14861              *         SCKW  PREVIOUS,SCNPREV,A
                                   14862              *         SCKW  FBLOCK,SCNFBLK,A
                                   14863              *         SCKW  LBLOCK,SCNLBLK,A
                                   14864              *         SCKW  *,SCNCURR
                                   14865              **IOWA*   SCKW  ATTN,SCNATTN,A
                                   14866              **IOWA*   SCKW  ATTENTION,SCNATTN,A
                                   14867              **IOWA*   SCKW  ABORT,SCNABORT,A
                                   14868              *         SCKW  ,,POP
                                   14869              *         SCKW  ,V(INVALID)

0                                  21900              * the dsname parameter scan routines are used by including
                                   21901              * a push pointer to dsnprt in the scan table for a command.
                                   21902              * these routines recognize group and user overrides. at the
                                   21903              * end of the scan of a line, the routine dsnfin completes
                                   21904              * processing of these parameters and must be called.
